- [ ] **FIX-2262**: Double booking vulnerability — check-then-act race condition
  - File: `backend\src\controllers\allotmentController.js`
  - Finding: F-2895
  - Use one of:
1. MongoDB findOneAndUpdate with conditions: findOneAndUpdate({ roomId, date, status: "available" }, { $set: { status: "booked" } })
2. Unique compound index on (roomId, date) to prevent duplicates at DB level
3. Pessimistic locking with a distributed lock (Redis SETNX)
4. Optimistic concurrency with a version field

- [ ] **FIX-2266**: Read-modify-write race condition in critical operation
  - File: `backend\src\controllers\bankAccountController.js`
  - Finding: F-2899
  - Use MongoDB atomic operators ($inc, $set) or wrap in a session/transaction with optimistic concurrency control (version field).
